Asqamu uniG n timuzɣa Mulud FERAǦUN
Mmis n igellil Ungal
Tasuqilt si tefransist
Mussa ǦULD TALEB
Tazwert n Yǧucef MERAHI Tazwert
Atan yewweḍ-ed lweqt anda temlal tasa d
win turew. S tezmert d waffud n Mussa Ǧuld
Taleb, ungal n Mulud Feraɛun, ”Mmis n igellil“,
yuɣal ar laṣel-is. Amek?
Ayen ɣef wayeg d-yemmeslay wungal agi d
tameddurt n weqbayli i yelḥan daxel uɣerbaz n
uṛumi, d ayen yeɣra, d ayen yeḍran d wamek
isebbel babas taṛwiḥt-is i wakken mmis - Furulu -a d-issukes tawacult-is si yir liḥala nni deg aydeg
ttidiren, d amek iwala lferq i yellan gar-as d uṛumi,
d amek yessaweḍ i wakken ad yelmed tamusni s
tutlayt tabeṛṛanit mebla ma yettu tutlayt ines tanaṣlit.
Mulud Feraɛun yeɣra geddac n yedlisen i
d-yefkan tamuɣli tucmitt ɣef tmetti tazzayrit. Mi ar
a nwali ayen d-uran fellaneɣ“les Gauthier d
Raymǧnd Martial”, a nefhem abrid n tira i yeḍfeṛ
wemyaru nneɣ i wakken a d-yesbin udem n tidett
n tɣerma n tmetti taqbaylit.
Asmi i d-yessuffeɣMulud Feraɛun ungal
agi ines s iṣurdiyen-is à cǧmttte d’auteur di “Les
Cahiers du nǧuḍel humanisme”, aṭas n yemyura
izzayriyen i s-yennan belli amyaru yagi iweǧǧeh
tamuɣli-s ala ɣer temnaṭ n tmurt n leqbayel;
nnan-as daɣen belli ungal agi yura-t bab-is i
lmend n iṛumyen mačči n izzayriyen. Ayagi mazal
a t-id-qaren aṛiḍa, maca Mulud Feraɛun
isbeggen-ed, s tutlayt i yessen nezzeh, s yiwen
uɣanib d afessas, tilawt n tmetti taqbaylit.
Assagi, s tsuqilt agi, Mǧussa Ǧuld Taleb
yefka tagnitt i yal yiwen degneɣi wakken a n ɣer,
neɣ a nεiwed taɣuri, s teqbaylit - tutlayt nneɣ tayemmatt - i wungal agi “Mmis n igellil”. Tutlayt i
yessexdem Ǧuld Taleb d taqbaylit nni timserreḥt,
i yezmer ad yefhem yal yiwen. Yessexdem diɣen
kra n wawalen imaynuten les nẓǧlǧgismes,
maca asexdem nnsen yella-d s tegzi d
tiḥṛci n tira. Dɣa di tagara n wedlis, Ǧuld Taleb
yefka-d yiwen n umawal amecṭuḥ i wakken ad
iεiwen ameɣri le lecteur.
Mass Mulud Feraɛun ilul di tefsut n 1913
u yettwanɣa, s ufus azeggaɣ, OAS, ass n 15 mars
1962 netta d xemsa yeṛfiqen-is. Yenna uqbel tamettant-is:
“Zemreɣad mmteɣass-agi neɣ ad ttwanɣeɣs ṛṣaṣ azekka. ḥṣiɣbelli bbiɣ-d aciddi deg yiwen
wegdud amnayfi i yesεan lhiba tameqrant ar a Yǧucef MERAHI Mulud Feraɛun Ixf I Tawacult
yeqqimen s lhiba tameqrant”.

a s-teεǧeb, ur yezmir wul-is ad yeqqim d
asemmaḍ. Tamuɣli ines d tin yessefṛaḥen, ccbaḥa
ines am ucewwiq yezzuzunen. Ɣef aya i seεεun
ciṭuḥ n leḥnana ɣef leεwayed imezdaɣ-is.
Ur yelli d zzux imi ulac tardast n tmurt ur
yedhin sser, yal tiɣilt tettak acbi ɣer weltmas, d
ccna yellan di ta i yellan di tahin. Ulac ssebba i

nnẓer akkmani anda nniḍen.

sεint ara ccan imi d-ttakent udem n tid yesqaccew imezdaɣ.

Mmis n igellil
Tehri n wezniq teqqim akken deg meḍqan
deg i yettwaẓeṛṛeb s leḥyuḍ deg yiwet n tama:
azal n setta iɣallen. Degmi d-bennun sya u sya,
ččan-as-d, dermen-d segs, kemnen-t, yettuɣaḍ di
lḥebs-is. Ad ikkuffer limmer ulac sya ɣer da,ɣef
yidisan-is, kra izerban issufuɣen ɣer lexlawi.
Amek i tebɣiḍ ad tbeddeḍ fell-as neɣ ad
telḥuḍ deg-s, wezniq yellan d azrib? Amek a s-tessuḍ, abrid nni xaṭi? Deg unebdu, ččuṛen d
aɣebbaṛ di sin, di tegrest yugar-it deg waluḍ imi d-ttemlilin akk deg-s lɣaci. Ɣef annect-agi daɣen i
yezga yumes. Ma d izerban nni ttaken acbiɣures
imi d arraw-is.
A nnmeyyez ger sin izerban yemqabalen,
yiwen yerra ɣef yeffus, wayeḍ yerra ɣef zelmeḍ.
Anda ma llan, yettimɣur wemḍiq-nni. Wissen d
zzheṛ yeffren isem-is, neɣ d lebɣi deg teswiεt-a ur
aɣtekfi ara ad tt-id-nessefru? Akken yebɣu yili,
imezwura nneɣ ur bnin ara din: aqli-kken-id deg
wemṛaḥ amuqran n taddart, “Amṛaḥ iḍebbalen”,
d win i d tajmaεt nneɣ . Ulac am nettat. Adrum
ufella ittasem deg-s.
Zzint-as-d teslaḍin s-ya u s-ya isenden ɣef
leḥyuḍ n yexxamen, ulint-ed ɣef lqaεa s lqedd
iḍaṛṛen n wemdan, tehri nnsent azal n sin iɣallen,
win ibɣun yeqqim fellasent, ama d argaz ama d
aqcic. Yiwet degsent tedduri. Deg
unebdu, ur tt-ikeččem yiṭij; di tegrest ur tt-ittḥaz
ugeffur. D tin i d taslaṭ yelhan imeṛṛa, temsel u
tecrureq; beqqun akk ad qqimen degs. Ma s-d-tekkeḍ s-ufella i tejmaεt, tin tezga-d ɣef zelmeḍ, tseqqef; Mulud Feraɛun lǧir; d imellalen, d
terra udem-is ɣer yiwet n tezribt yesεan lewhi n
εecrin n lmitrat d-iqqeṛṛeε yiwen wexxam.
Taddart tebḍa ɣef tlata iderma, yal adrum s
tejmaεt-is, yal tajmaεtɣures tidekkanin n yeẓra d
teslaḍin imeslen. Akkmani tiddas llant, ttujeṛḍent
ɣef teslaḍin. Maca yiwen ur yezmir a d-yini tella
tejmaεt yifen “amṛaḥ iḍebbalen”.
Llan diɣen sin leǧwamaε. Maca, ur yuli ara
ccan nnsen am tjemmuyaε. Si beṛṛa ma tent-waliḍ, kifkif-iten d tizeɣwa i tent-id-isuman. D acu,
zzdaxel, tiɣerɣert nnsen temsel, leḥyuḍ nnsen selɣen s ilmawen, d
isemmaḍen. Imɣaren yettẓallan din amzun akken
kkan-d di leqrun nni n zik.
Lqahwa tezga-d di beṛṛa n taddart, di laεzib.
Win yebɣan ad iṛuḥ, ilaq-as ad yeffeɣakin i tnezduɣin.
Kra n tnezduɣin ulint-ed melmi kan s lmend
n uṣurdi d-yettwaḥellan di Fṛansa. Ssufɣent-ed
udem nnsent amaynut akk d lqermud nnsent
azeggaɣger ufercec n tiyaḍ. Cemtent, nfaq s
ulameɣnni d uzlig. Tugna nnsent ur teltiɣ ɣer tin n
taddart.
Tabaε yiwen ur yecrih yissent. 
Mebεid ttbanent-ed am ccwami timellalin ireggmen di
tyessetmatin nnsent igan s wakal. Neẓra zdaxel
gant am tidak akk nniḍen. Uklalent aεekki:
“Adaynin n Mnayel s-ufella mellul d acebḥan,
zdaxel yeččuṛ d leɣber d isredyan”.
Zzux ttiεewji i deg nekkat yak, nekṛeh win
yessemɣaren iman-is, ahat imi nettemyili i meṛṛa.
Mmis n igellil : ttemyerḍalen,
Ɣef akken d-qqaren, imezwura nneɣ dduklen s tmara. Ṛṛwan lmerta n tudert n “yal wa i
yiman-is” iwakken a s-d-ssuksen kra neɣ kra i
tdukli. ẓidet tmeddurt ma yilin lǧiran, acku ttemḥamin, ttemyafen
ttemsaεafen. Ssifsusen taεkwemt; akken tebɣu
tili ccedda ma ra s-zzin rennu-tt. Ttagwaden ṭṭiq
am tmettant, keṛhen-tt am qeḍran. Tikwal yettili
akka cwiṭ umennuɣ, cwiṭ n leεyaḍ ger kra ɣef lmal
ma yekcem tafarka n yiwen,ɣef llufanat, atg…
Maca ferrun mi ara yili lfeṛḥ neɣ lqeṛḥ. Neqqar: “D
lǧiran i rreḥma mačči i nneqma”. Ṛṛeḥma nneɣ , d
ṛṛeḥma n ddunit maca mačči d times.
Ɣas akken yal adrum yekka-d seg yiwen
uẓar, ulac fellas, imi yiwen ur yettarra ddehn-is ɣer wannect-a. Si zik ttilint tmeɣriwin ger iderma.
Ass-a amezruy n taddart yuɣal amzun n yiwen
wemdan. Ulac win d-yufraren s-nnig wayeḍ.
Nettfeṭṭin garaneɣkra yellan. Izlan, icewwiqen
ttmucuha sduklen asaḍen nneɣ : ama yella d
amẓiw am waɣzen, d ushil am Bṛiṛuc neɣ d uḥṛic am Ǧeḥḥa.
Limmer ad-neddem adrum at wadda, a t-naf yekka-d seg yiwen umi qaren Maẓuz. Wagi
yeǧǧa-d seddus n warrac. Frurxen, fkan-d xemsa
n twaculin, yal yiwet tebbi isem n wergaz, zzdint d
Sliman, At Musa, At Lεeṛbi akk d At qasi. Ma d
Ibaciren, jedditsen d imenfi d-yusan si Ǧeṛǧeṛ.

iɣ-yewwten”. 
Ur d-yettban yiwen ur d-yecliε degsen, ula d nutni ttmeyizen amzun kkan-d si Maẓuz. 
Tikwal ma tibrik tegnitt neɣ ma yil ubaɣur di tqaεett, yettili win sen-d-yessekkefalen tiqdimin.
S nnig iẓuran agi yellan zik d yiwen nneɣ iɣ-yesduklen ass-a, Leqbayel imesdurar yiwet lḥala
nnsen, yiwet tmeddurt nnsen. “Yiwen uεekkaz igellil wala akk ameṛkanti.
D tidett llan sin yeswiren n tmeddurt: anda
llan wid yufan iman nnsen: ččan - swan - lsan; d
wanda wid, ass-a aten-id-iwali yiṭij, ass-a aten-id-idel wagu. Yeskeεbubuc-iten laẓ, yettsumu
degsen, izeggi-ten am yifer. Ttawḍen ɣer lqaε n
lbir, ttɣaḍen bab nnsen yettwali-ten-id. Maca ur
yezmir yiwen ad ibḍu garasen neɣ ad ifaq i tmeẓla
nnsen s umata.
Imeṛkantiyen d wid yesεan tiferkiwin:
azemmur, tineqqlin, azal n xemsa wussan n
tyerza d waman di tferka-s i tebḥirin. Di tejmaεt
ma d-addren lɣella n yiwen mi ara d-yaweḍ lawan
n tyerza, yettban-ed wa yecṛeh wudem-is, wa
amzun yesqeḍ neɣ yusem. D acu, deg-ceṛfan
nneɣ , yibbwas n tyerza s tyuga n yezgaren,
yugaren cwiṭ kan akraren, drus n wakal. Amuqran
deg meṛkantiyen n Leqbayelɣures azal n waggur n
tyerza. Yessuzur taɣuct-is di tejmaεt, amzun deg-wexxam-is i yella. Akka i yɣil, lɣaci teddun-as di lebɣi.
Iwakken as-fken leqder wa d isεu lhiba, imi
d tigi id-yettbanen di trika-s, yettak leεtab i yiman-Mmis n igellil
is am win wer nesεi tabruyt. Mi ara yawi imestujaṛ,
ixeddem annect nnsen, yettlusu am nutni, itett
garasen anagar iɣublan ur ibeṭṭu yara yidsen.
Ad tafeḍɣures lmal: tayuga n yezgaren,
tafunast, kra n wakraren d wulli, aɣyul neɣ aserdun.
Tanezduɣt-is tezmer ad tesεu sin yexxamen
mqabalen lewhi n ṭnac iɣallen di tehri d rbaεṭac di

ubeɣli n wakal, ssqef s uɣanim d lqeṛmud.
Tiɣerɣert tessun-as talaɣt, zzuzuren-as s ufella
ibruyen n lǧir d cwiṭ n win yufafen, tedzentt
mmzintt. Ma tili akken d tamaynutt tettecruruq,
yettcebbiḥ wexxam. Ma d leḥyuḍ selɣent-tten
tilawin ukessar, azal n sin iɣallen ɣef lqaεa, s lǧir yemzin,
rennunt-as yiwen uzirig qqaren-as
taεmamt, ula d win s lǧir maca ur yemzi yara; ma

i sen-t-ilaqen alama cerwent-ett
merriɣet, acku d ccɣel nnsent, yuɣal asent tikwal
d aɣbel tikwal d iseɣ. Aslaɣyettnalas yal aseggas

Tanezduɣt nneɣ tezga-d deg-ixef ugafa n

Remḍan, wayeḍ Lewnis maca deg wedrum Mulud Feraɛun

a d-yini: « ulac win d-teǧǧa tɣalaṭ ». Di tazwara,

uɣalen d irgazen. Isem ten yezdin iḥeṛṛem-iten

ɛemmi, umi sawaleɣbaba Lewnis yesεa taksumt d rrqiq wudem-is.

s uqendur amellal d waεmam yenneḍɣef uqerru-s

Mmis n igellil
Iban am yiṭij uzal belli d netta i tḥemmel aṭas.
Tefka-yas tafekka ackitt. D tin i d tarzeft-is tamezwarut. Tesbanay-ed
iman-is di mmis
amenzu: acmumeḥ, udem, taɣuct yiwen nnsen.
Remḍan di tama nniḍen yettemcabi swa
swa ar Caεban. D lmektub, ahat, i yebɣan att
isebbeṛ imi s-d-yefka ger ifassen-is ayen i s a-ywali udem n babas. D allal ushil swayes a d-yesmektay win t-id-yeǧǧan. Remḍan d imsibrik
ciṭuḥ, yeǧhed, wezzil yerna zzur ɣef gmas. Akken i
d afellaḥ n tmurt nneɣ , yebren u yekkunner. « Ma
d udem-is d Caεban kkes-it ffer-it » i d-teqqar

tireqqaqin d leḥnak. Yesεa anexzuṛ n babas d
yiwet n lεadda, iteqqen tiṭ tazelmaṭ ma k-id-imiqel. Asmi yella meẓẓi, ayen teεreḍ setti as-tekkes lεadda nni, εeddi keč. Tikli ines d taẓayant
iḍaṛṛen mfarraεen. Mi yefka
am tin n yilef
aqqeddim a s-tiniḍ d amennuɣi ɣer iteddu, neɣ ɣer taεkumt a tt-id-yerfed. Setti terra-t am ubelbul
kan ur n neṭṭeq ur n smenṭaq, ur yelli d win
icerḍen. Mačči d ačeqlal am gmas. D asusam u d

ẓẓay ula di lecɣal-is. Amzun tura deg wengir-is
tfellaḥt, netta daɣen iqbel-itt. Xas akken zzur-it

D acmamaḥ, rnuɣures lehduṛ n Mulud Feraɛun

Asmi d-luleɣ, εemmi d tikli a d-yessiweḍ
xemsin iseggasen di lεemṛ-is, baba ṛebεin. Ɣursen
di sin dderya.
ḥlima, tameṭṭut n εemmi, n at ufella. D
tameṭṭut tačaṛant, d tuwεiṛt u zuret taɣuct-is.
Allen-is berqent u tikli ines am wemcic. Bih-bih,
teɣḍel-ed lbeq ɣef setti, almi itt tetthabi, tuɣal-as d
izem deg wexxam. Yeεyu yekkat-itt baba
Lewnis, akken tugi a tterr aḍar, ur tettaggad
yiwen. Acengu ines d baba, tekṛeh-it am dda,
limmer tettaf ur tt-tettwali yara imi ifaq i txidas-is.
Akken ma nella deg wexxam neẓra belli tebbi
daεwessu n temɣart-is,ɣef ayagi i s-nettawi u
nettbibbi timerẓuga ines.
Yerna d setti i tt-id-ixeḍben. Babas n ḥlima,
yellan d amddakul n jeddi, yedda d aεsekṛiw ɣer tmurt
iberkanen. Mi d-yuɣal di Madaɣecqer,
yebbi-d yides adrim. Setti tɣill-it d amerkanti, tufa
uɣur a tsenned cwiṭ arraw-is. Teffeɣ-as tirga
mxalfa, tamsalt texdem tendem degs. Amɣar
amcum yerked di nṣib n yellis, ur yerni ara cwiṭ
yesssufeɣtaṛwiḥt. D acu id-yeǧǧa? yiwet n cciεa
iṛuccen s wewraɣyurez usekref n leḥrir azegzaw,

tqendyar-is. S ijerbuben i tebɣa at-teqqim. Ur
tɛaṭṭel ara tessenger weltmas acku mi qqaḥsent
tqwendyar s d-tečča nana meskint ur s d-yeggri
wara, u baba ur yessaweṛ ara a s-d-yaɣ tiyaṛ. Tin ɣers, tuɣal t-talexxaxt nettat yellan zeddiget:
tteffeɣ anda tettɣimi, tettaggad aman am tmes u
wer tettanef i yiwen a s-yemceṛ. Werčin yumis
wexxam nneɣ am ussan agi ineggura. Ayen
yessewhamen di xalti t-tadawsa ines: tettcuffu,
yettizwiɣ wudem-is u tettuzur taɣwect-is. Ayen d-yeɣlin n lqut ger ifassen-is tessɛadda-t, aɣunfu
tennuɣ yides. Tuɣal am tileft ma d leɛqel yezga
yunag. Ma d yemma meskint tecrew, ala agwlim
i d-yeggran degs. Tɣaṛ medden ɣef yeɣsan
meḥḥa maca lemɣiṛat ula i ɣ-d-gent. Tura ɣef
yiman nneɣ i nettru mačči ɣef xalti. Nettnadi
tifrat, akken tebɣu tili neɣ ansi tebɣu tekk-ed, ɛidet.
Zrin kra n wussan, xalti tuɣal ters. Truṣ am
tin yekkawen, tefcel. Deg wexxam kksen-as cced.
Degmi a yali was, nettat t-tiɣimit deg yiwet n
tdekkant ddaw useqqif. Allen unagent, tettargu s
ibeddi. Tilkin yulin ɣef i jerbuben-is d uqerruy-is
ttqeggilent i yiṭij aṣmayan n tegrest. Ur ilaq wa tt-Mulud Feraɛun
Zemreɣ a d-iniɣ belli baba
ilaɛin neɣ wa tt-imassen. Yemma tenna-k t-talemmast n wagur i d-isersen talwit di weltmas.
Tkukra fellas a tt-id-yuɣal werway nni ines di
tagara neɣ di tlalit n wagur amaynut. Ma t-tičiratin
skerkisent: nnant-as belli d lečnun i ykecmen
xalti; sya ɣer zdat at-tuɣal at-tetkacef u a d-tessis yettak
ayen a s a tidir twacult di liser.
tameɛɛuɣt u westewtew n temɣarin seg wakken
ṣercawet ddunit. Ma d yemma trekkem seg
wurfan, ur s-yefki yara wul-is at-tfaḥes deg ubaxix
yuɣen weltmas. Ur tettanef ara i yiwet di yessis n
ḥmed at-tuɣal t-taseṣṣart neɣ t-tamkaceft. I ɛideṛ
a lṣif! Menyif tamettant n tmeslubt! a s-yeddun di
lebɣi d aggay n weltmas ɣer yemḥabṛen a s-d-arun neɣ s alebɛaṛ n lemqamat a s-ssufɣen
lečnun. Ɣas, tamezwarut, ur tettamen ara aṭas s
lecyax, tis snat ur yeshil ara ɣef baba ad yawi
yides tameslubt. Laqen yedrimen, amerkub,
imṣamiyen, ad yečč axxam t-tferka, ad yeṣbes
lxwedma,… Mačči d yiwet; Taggara tin d-iseqfen
sufella ɣef tikli ger iberdan d lɛtab d umesruf,
xalti rqiq ṭmaɛ n ṣellu-s aṭas aṭas.
Degmi ters cwiṭ xalti, At Musa uɣalen lhan-d
d ccɣel nnsen am zik. Ger lmerta n ddunit d
iɣeblan nnsen, imarawen nneɣ ttun tameslubt
yettidiren garasen, ttmektin-tt-id kan ma tili zdat
wallen nnsen. Tuɣal d aɛggal nniṛen deg wexxam.

- Anef-iyi a d-ɛreɣ weltma, i yi-d-tenna.
ɛarṛent tulawin a tt-id-sneṭqent ulac. Ma fkant-as-d talqwimt n weɣrum neɣ takwemmict n iniɣman

yiwet n tmeddit, Faṛma, Baya d ḥemdan mi d-usan di lexla ur d-ufin ara xalti deg wexxam. Titi

lɛacra, bɣiɣ a t-id-rreɣ s axxam.
imeṭṭawen mi s-d-ṣkiɣ. Almi d assen i d-tuder
xalti weltmas yemmuten. 
D tt-id-yettuɣalen? Imi timeqbert tezga-d akin kan cwiṭ i

tt-naf ɣer tama uɛekka n nana. tenna-k yemma
din kan a tili, maca yiwen ur yexliq di tmeqbert.
Deg wezrib daɣen ulac.
Azal n ssaɛa nekwni d anadi ɣef xalti almi s
d-yenna yiwen umeksa i baba belli iwala-tt mi
tɛub s Amalu.
Amalu t-taferka d-yečča jeddi ḥmed i yessis
di tlata. Degs azemmur d lexrif. Tezga-d deg
uzaɣar ukessar, igezm-itt yiwen yeɣɛer, yedrem u
yal ma wwten waman yettaṣmal-d. Tabriṭ
yettawin ɣures tenneṛ, yezzi-yas-d sya u sya yinijel
t-tidekt aṭubbu ɣures azal n wezgen n ssaɛa ma d
alluy tɛedda ssaɛa. Tafsut t-tafsut u t-tikli a d-yeɣli yiṛ. Kkawen ifadden n baba tessaɛwej tyerza
n kra yekka was, yessewɛaḥ a tt-yehnu alma d i Mulud Feraɛun
Amalu a d-yerr xalti.
Darani tura ters. Meḥḥa nɣil at-tens deg uɛacciw
deg ttaǧǧant xwalti asaɣur iwakken a t-zzenzent.

Yemma s timmad-is akka i tmeyyez. Wiɛran?

uqerru n tmeslubt? Neɣ d iɣilifen a d-yuɣalen?
Deg wexxam, ɣas nenneɣwni cwiṭ nestehza
daɣen aṭas. Lṣaṭun, nwet akw nneṣ, yiwen ur tt-yekcim weɣbel.
Tignawt n Meɣres ttetti am tata; d ayen i
yeṛran deg yiṛ nni: ixeṭr-d lṣal deg yiwet n teswiɛt.
Ageffur yekkat s uzayaṛ, aṛu yebɣa ad yessifeg
lqermud ula ɣer ger lecqayeq n lelwaṣ yettsuṛu-d.
Yemma terra-d weltmas ger wallen-is, tkecm-itt
tergagit. Ayen yeɛreṛ baba a s-yekkes aɣbel
tegguma. Ula d netta ur yerkid ara, rnu ineɛmi n

yelsa lqecc-is yeffeɣ. Nesla-yas mi s-yessawal i
gmas. Rran di sin ssakwin-d kra n laɛmum usan-d
s axxam zzin d agraw. Ahat di xemsa neɣ di setta
yidsen i llan.
icifad, nnṛen deg yebrenyas Meḥḥa

Mmis n igellil

waɛlaw, yeṭṭes di teɣmert. Taṭṭucin n yemma t-tizeggwaɣin deg meṭṭi, ur ufin ara xalti. Deg
wassen ur tṛal tiṭ nneɣ fellas i yiwen deg wexxam
ur yeɛri amek i d-as-teṛra i tmeɣbunt. Ma d nek
cukkeɣ d iɣɛer umalu i t-yeččan.
Deg uzaɣar n Tizi Wezzu, asif n Taxuxt d
iɣeɛran d-yemlalen din zgan ssusufen-d widan
wwin. Tafekka umeɣbun ččan att-tafeṛ tezzegzew,
aɛebbuḍ yeqbeḥ deg waman icuf am teylut, allen
fɣent-ed, imi yelli, iles yeɛluleq. Wissen lbext n
xalti ma akken i s-iga at-tekfu ussan-is? Yiwen
mačči yeɛra. Ma yafen medden yiwen lmegget
iṛegger-it-id wasif ɣer rrif-is, ad ssufɣen awal, ad
yelṣu ɣef tuddar, a d-asen lɣaci a t-walin. Ma
nnsen a t-awin s axxam-is ad ɛiwzen fellas a t-neṭlen azekka nni, ma wer taɛqilen ara ad
yettwanṭel wissen amek di tmurt taberranit.
Tabaɛ d akal n ḥebbi yakk. Ma d imawlan-is a t-aysen.
Akken i d aɣ-teṛra i nekwni. Dduḥt meḥḥa d
anadi ɣef xalti, later-is ur iban. Ula d aṭubbu ines
s Amalu yuɣal di ccek, acku ameksa nni ur yeṭṭif
ara deg wawal-is degmi yesla i tulawin fkant-as
udem nniṛen. Ur d-gireɣ ara axerriṛ ɣef xalti mi s-d-nniɣ i yemma walaɣ-tt zdat lakul mi terra ɣer
tmeqbert; seg imiren yal wa taɣwect d-yettawi:
Tameslubt meskint tɣab, tuɣal am lmalayekkat,
tezger di ddunit ɣer laxert, teṛfer weltmas amzun
tbeddek kan axxam. Wid yettmeyyizen ur sen-gin Mulud Feraɛun
ara ccan i ymennan agi, ur sen-kcimen sya ur sen-ffiɣen sya. Yemma tejreṣ tasa-s acku werɛad yeṣli
udeddic n tmettant n nanna mi tendef s twaɣit
yeglan s xalti.
Ma nniɣ-d netru aṭas xalti, skadbeɣ, acku
deg wasmi temmut nanna amzun akken leḥzen
yezga deg wexxam nneɣ, yezdeɣ degneɣ u
yettidir yidneɣ, rnu iɣeblan d iɛakkkiḥen n yal
ass. Limmer an-nerr tasa d lemɣiṛat di rrif nezmer
a d-nini belli neɛya di tegnitt deg nella u nessaram
ciṭuṣ n liser t-tmendit. Ala yemma i s-iṣulfan mliṣ
i tyita yagi taneggarut. Tenna-k yerreɛ ufurek
aneggaru n twacult  ahbuh… afurek useklu iwet
maras -, ur d-yeggri uɛar wuɣur a terzu neɣ a d-yerzun fellas, ur tesɛi yiwen nniṛen ṣala ḥebbi d
wexxam n wergaz-is akked laṣnana n dderya-s.
Tikwal tettlummu deg yiman-is, teqqar stehzeɣ di weltma.
Nekkni s imecṭaṣ nfaq belli truṣ tɣawsa
yesɛan azal ameqwran: taxxamt n xwalti.

garas d wexxam is. Taferka nni tamcumt ur

idrimen-is. Dayen… Yensa ucewwiq n

nusim di dduṣ, tɣum teṛwiqt n tafat deg Ixf II Amenzu

weqcic amur-is i dadda-s, yella win a s-d-ikecmen degs!

Atta twacult Nat Musa. Di sebɛa yidsen. Yiwen i
d-yessasayen aɣrum. D babatsen. Ihebber am yilef, ur s-yettḥuṣ yiwen wass, itekkes-itt i tɛabbuṭ-is yettak-it i
warraw-is, iɛemd agus almi d ulamek, ur yettṛeggir ur
yettanef i win a yṛegren. Yettergigi i laɛyudat i sekfuyen
adrim, yettaggad tagrest i tetten deg kufan. Furulu, gmas
d yessetmas kren-d akken wɛan. S umata, ur tulwa yara
tudert nnsen, tin wer d-nečči lateḥ di tqerrut n Furulu,
maca yir tiswiɛin yessɛadda di temɛi-s yettwali-tent am di lemri.
Ɣures ṣdac iseggasen asmi yeffeɣ babas d amuṛin
seg wakken yefka dderk i yiman-is s lxedma. T-taggara n
lexḥif, uṛan akk n ḥemṛan di lexla yettqaraɛ idenyen n
tazert. Mi d-tufrar tafat a d-yali s axxam. Yiwet n tikkelt Mulud Feraɛun
yusa-d udem-is weḥḥaɣ, allen-is nexḥent, ssuḥa-s teṣma.
Yesres tacekkaḥt n weslen d-yemṣelfaf ɣef waɛrur-is,
yerra ad yeṭṭes.
Ɣiwel ssu-yas-d, del-it, rnu-yas tasumta. Lqut rɛag deg
yimi-s, d iṛes kan. Tameṭṭut-is tɣil a s-iɛeddi, yessis

temsalt yesbeṛ. Tabaɛ babas yečhed, yezmer i dderk
netta, mačči d cwiṭ n waṭṭan a t-iɣeṛlen.

tqarɛeṛ iniɣman iṛ-a? Axxi a k-id-walin medden! id-yessakwi!

Deg wexxam, yufa-d yiwen ccix a yettaru lṣerz.
Babas yella yeṭṭes, d amḥabed nni i t-id-yessakwin.
Yesteqsa-t, Remṛan yenna-yas-d amek teṛra yides.
Iban d lečnun i t-ikecmen. Di lɛinser, seddaw
wennar, i ttwawṛen deg yiṛ ur iɛabbed yiwen degsen.
Ayen d-yusan s ɣursen ɣef demma n umuṛin. Tura,
iwakken a t-fɣen, tlaq tazla idammen uqelwac akw d
ubexxer s ifarrawen ilili yura ufus n ṭṭaleb di snat
tamiwin. Tlata tikkal n ubexxer u yal abrid s yiwen yifer.
Akken ur ɛarqen ara deg farrawen, yal yiwen iɛarreb-it
ccix s yiwen, s sin d tlata ijeḥḥiden.
limmer a ten-inamer!
Yemmekta-d tamacahutt sen-d-iwet ccix di lakul,
i deg, iwakken ad yeddu di lebɣi i yemmas yettṣellilen
degs a s-d-yaru lṣerz ɣer wemḥabeṛ, yeddem-d iccer n
Lečnun ɣeṛlen-d rrehba di Furulu, a sen-yecfu Mulud Feraɛun
lkaɣeṛ yaɛṛef s lemṣadra yura degs asefru n Si muṣ u
Mṣend. Annect-a, akken a d-yini i yessetmas belli netta
yeɣra u yefhem; Tikerkas n bu taɛmamt ten-yeɛgen s

tamacahutt nni u yenna-yasent-id belli asefru n Si muṣ u
Mṣend yessaṣla tamɣart nni ugar n lṣerz n wemḥabeṛ.
Maca ur t-ssawṛent ara tissas-is a tt-id-yeṣku zdat ṭṭaleb
d-yuran llṣerz neɣ skud ur yeṭṭis ara babas, acku ma d-yakwi umuṛin, ma k-id-yesmuqul, wiɛran ma d netta neɣ
d lečnun t-izedɣen i k-id-yeččan s wallen? Ahat a ten-id-nnfeṣ a d-uɣalen ɣurek? Di teswiɛin am tigi i yebɣu
yecnu ccix n lakul aɛbaḥ-is ur yeṭṭerdiq ara; Furulu yerra

yehwa-yas kan iɣeṛl-ed ɣef yiman-is aḥɛiɛec, ggumman
lečnun ad fɣen bab nnsen.
Yusa-d wemḥabeṛ wis sin, yerna-d wis tlata maca
yiwen nnsen, ulac win d-yeglan s ṣellu. Ma d-yakki
Remṛan, ad ifaq d yiman-is, yeqqar-asen-d belli ur t-yezdiɣ wara, maca ma s-tesleṛ yettlejlij, yewɛar a s-tiniṛ ulac-iten degs.

neɣ sin yezmer ad yebṭel yiwen wass ad yeks leṣq-is.

tili taɣaṭ am ta!
Imeksawen mačči ala tayessawt i ten-yeggunin,

uzemmur d alqaṛ, di lawan iniɣman daɣen akken,

yessetmas timeqranin di baṭel. Ur iṛur yiwen ma yruṣ ɣer
lakul. Yemmas d yessetmas ṭṭfen-t lexla d wexxam, babas
yezga yettcegiɛ-d xemseṭṭac neɣ ɛacrin alef i tučwin n
temɛin, babas Lewnis iqeṭṭu-d di ssuq ayen ilaqen i wexxam.
Di lawan n uzemmur kan i yettasem cwiṭ deg wid
d-yeffɣen di lakul. D igelfan n ɛɛerzur d umergu i d-iɣellin ɣef tzemrin. Mi ara d-lhin yergazen d wecraw,
tilawin d welqaṛ, imeksawen, nitni, ttarantt i tanduyt.

ɣures mitin, teltmeyya, llan wid yessawṛen xems-meyya.

tent-id-ttɛassan. Ad ssiɣen times ad ssaṣmun ifassen

yaɛluleq deg useṛru. Ifrax nni ad mmezlen, ad necwen u
ad ččaren yissen tiqelmunin nnsen; ma d wid d-ttaṭafen
timeddiyin n wass ttawin-ten-tid s axxam d imudduren.

ɣursen ttmagaren-ten s wannecten n yefrax akken a ten-sseqṛen.

di lakul. Irekkem seg urfan ma ywali wwin-as taqellaɛt d

yettṣiri a d-yas wagur n Meɣres a deg a tekfu tanduyt
akked welqaṛ uzemmur.

yenṭer ma t-tura ccwi-t. D ḥebbi ur nebɣi yara ad
yesgujjel arraw-im di babatsen.
Aqcic d yemmas uɣalen s axxam ṣeznen. Mi d-usant teqcicin di lexla mlalen-d meḥḥa, zzin ɣef lkanun.
Ulawen ččuren, udmawen cerwen. Tikwal, tseffeṛ allen-is Faṛma s ijifeḥ n tmeṣremt-is. Ula d imeṭṭi s tufra,
ammer lčiran ad ɛren tawaɣit yuɣen axxam n ḥemdan.
Tameddit n wass i d-yekcem Dda Lewnis.
Yewwi-d isalen s usefruri. Yebɣa ad yekkes anweɣni i
warraw n gmas. Ula d netta ur iris ara lxaṭer-is yaɛni!
Isawel tidett Aɛmer? Ulac d acu yeffer? Faṛma tettṣellil
deg ulwes-is a s-d-yini ayen yeɛra. Netta yettgalla ar
gmas ar yeṣla, ar ulac i t-yuɣen, fiṣel ma rnan-d aɣbel
wer nelli. Yebɣa ad yawi arrac, di sin, ad ččen imensi
ɣures. Faṛma tugi, yeffeɣ s wurfan. Yuli-ten yakk wurrif
d uɣilif. Qebren ɣer daxel, tuqaɛ-asen am tyersi di
tgerjumt. Tabratt ur tesɛiṛ i d-tssefra: “Idrimen i wen-nefkiɣ cuṣet-asen ciṭuṣ. Ur sɛiɣ d acu a wen-n-rnuɣ,
ṭebret kra n waguren. Ma twalam ur kken-tqaddan ara,
zzenzet taɣaṭ d yiwen useklu...”.
Azekka nni di lakul, yessefra-yasen-d ccix yiwen
weṛris: “Ulac i yɛiden am temɛi. Kunwi s warrac n
lakul, ur tesɛim d acu i kken-iceɣben nnig taɣuri d wurar.
Iḍes nnwen fessus, ur yelli cwal a t-yerwin, ur yelli
wayen a kken-yesneɣnin. Tikwal babatwen yettruṣu-yas
Mmis n igellil yiṛes iṛ meḥḥa, ttemseṛfarent-d tlufa t-yezzan yiwet yiwet ger wallen-is. Yetterkab-it wurrif, yettergigi ɣef dderya-s,
yettkukru imeṭṭulba a t-ṣerṭen, yettaggad ikufan ad
qqimen d ilmawen. Kunwi ur kken-yerzi weɣbel, ɣurwen
ur teqris ur tmal; timsal teddunt s liser. “Xati! Ur teɛriṛ
tabruyt! i s-yeqqar Furulu deg ul-is ma akken d-yettmeslay ccix. Yebɣa a s-yini tamsirt agi inek tebna ɣef
tkerkas. Ula d arrac tjerreṣ tasa nnsen, beṭṭun tilufa n
Zrin kra n wussan, yeffeɣ wawal ɣef ḥemdan di
taddart, simmal ileṣṣu yettiɣzif u simmal yettiɣzif
gezmen-as aṛar, waqila di sin; kra qqaren-d yedderɣel,
wiyaṛ yemmut maṛi. Yuɣal dda Lewnis iṭub ɣer Tizi-Wezzu iceyyeɛ ddibic ɣer usensu anda yezdeɣ gmas. Bih-bih yuɣal-ed, tṛeffer-it-id tebratt. Aḥumi ur t-terri tmara a Mulud Feraɛun
d-yeskiddeb. Almi d akken i d-ters talwit deg wexxam.
Aseggwas d wezgen i n-yeqqim ḥemdan di
Fḥansa. Yiwet n tmeddit umezwaru n lexḥif, Furulu netta
d gmas uɣalen-d di lexla, nehḥen-d tajlibt n tɣeṭṭen. Mi t-tikli a d-awṛen taddart mlalen-d ḥsen, mmis n xal nnsen.
Yewwi aɣyul-is a t-id-yessew. ḥsen yekna ɣer Dadaḥ
yebbi-t di teṣnakt-is yenna-yas:
- Azzel, zwir gmas s axxam, yusa-d babak.
Arrac bedden di tlemmast n webrid am wid
iseḥɛen; llin allen nnsen d iqemmac nnsen, ggugmen.

yettmaṣṣinen deg yiman-is akken a t-id-yeqṛaɛ.

Mmis n igellil
Iṣar Furulu melmi a fɣen lɣaci akken a d-yeqqim

yettemṣelfaf s waccaren-is d wuglan-is netta t-tnelli

tebɣa a t-id-testixxer. Ssekren ččaqlala d laɛyaṛ almi d-gren imeqranen.
Kra n win yesɛan win s-yettilin di Lttari

t-yerṣan tura d anadi d beṭṭu n lqec d-yusan di Fḥansa.

lakul, d acu mačči zdat medden.
akked cwiṭ n lqec.

nnsent smeṣsisent i ymarrawen nnsent.
I tikkelt tis snat i d-yessefra ḥemdan amek i s-teṛra. I wakken a d-rren lbal nnsen warraw-is ɣef wayen

yeɣlin ɣef babak. Âer ansi d-yekka d wanda d-yuɣal.

ccama i d-yeggran.

yeɣra. D lekwaɣeṛ n wexxam n ccraɛ n temdint n “La seine”.

- Teɛriṛ? Ur zmiren ara a s-kelxen i babak, i s-yenna ḥemdan. Xeṭreɣ ccraɛ tikkelt tamezwarut, maca
rrɛiɣ-t, ur iɛedda yara felli uzaylal. Muqel tura ayen d-wwiɣ.
Ayɣer yexṭer abrid amezwaru u ayɣer yerɛa
ccraɛ? Di lluzin deg i ssefsayen uzzal i yxeddem
ḥemdan, maca am akken di tmurt n Leqbayel i yella, lqanun,
yettak dderk deg iman-is am akken t-yettak di tferka-s, aṣbas ulac.
ixeddem yal ass, ula d ass n lṣed ur yestaɛfuy ara. Ladɣa,
ass n lṣed i yuɣ tiɣrit. Yennesr-ed yiwen uceryun n
wuzzal iṣerṭ-it ɣer lṣiṛ. Yekcem ɣer sbiṭar n tkkebbanit.
Lčerṣ ur d-iban fellas maca yuɣ-itent zdaxel, teqreṣ
tegguma a s-tekkes. Tezzi-d ddurt, amejjay yenna-yas
ffeɣ teṣliṛ. D ayagi i ɣer yessaram ḥemdan. Iṣar a d-yawi
adrim, ad yerr attalasi ines u ad yuɣal s arraw-is.
Azekka nni yehna-tt ɣer lluzin. Tameddit mi yekfa
lxedma yusa-d ɣer texxamt-is, ssiṣ yuɣal-it-id, tgezzem
tɛabbuṭ-is a s-tiniṛ d ijenwiyen i yettcarrigen degs. Rran-t ɣer sbiṭar nniṛen, qrib yemmut. Din llin-as aɛbbuṛ-is.
Yeqqim-n tlata waguren ger tudert t-tmettant. Iɣeblan,
aṭan, acedhi n dderya rnu lweṣc n tmurt taberranit.
Asmi yesteqsa ɣer tkebbanit a s-d-txelleṭ ussan
nni yeqqim am akken ten-tettxelliṭ i wid yuṛnen,
tegguma. Iwala ččan-as taṣadra yessufeɣ-as-d lkarṭa. Kra
n “lmumnin”, ɣef wudem n ḥebbi akked lmɣiṛat, ṣuman-t, mlan-as-d amek a yexdem, ssekken-as-d sani a yerr
tid yellan di Mulud Feraɛun
Iwakken a d-iṣelli annect-a ḥemdan, ilaq-as
akken a d-yawi leṣq-is. Yeḥwa tazliwin, kkawen ifadden-is deg wṭubbu d walluy, taggara yewwi-d azref-is,
yerbeṣ ccraɛ. Xelleṭ-asen-d kra yeqqim u yerna-d s ufella
abursyun ɣef wer yegmin. Limmer yeɛri Furulu tadyant
iɛaddan ɣef babas, limmer yesli tamacahutt yeṛran yides,
yali a d-yemmeslay fellas asmi yesɛedda amzazwer u a d-yehdeḥ ɣef tlufa d-yemmuger babas akk t-tseɣlit t-yebṛan
netta d wid yeɣran, ad llin iqemmac nnsen wid a yeɣren aṛris-is!
Tilufa n ḥemdan d ayen yezrin, kfan-t. Ayen
iɛeddan iɛedda. Tenna-yas-d Faṛma menyif akka wala
ugar, u aṭan agi inek yusa-d di leṭlaṣ. Akken llan deg
wexxam ddan-d deg-wawal-is imi d-mmaren yedrimen
ɣef yiwet n tikkelt: telt-meyyat alef.
aseggas nniṛen n yinig.
Ass-a atan ger warraw-is d iɛeggalen-is, xas ixaṛ
uɛebbuṛ-is yeččur-d lčib-is. D ameḥkanti; Tura ad yerr
ayen s-ttalasen medden u ad yidir s liser. Qrib amelyun di
texriṭ-is! Ma d ccema-s a s-tt-yeṛmen ubursyun ines

Imejjayen nnan-as-d ilaq-ak at-teččeṛ mliṣ u a s-ternuṛ tiɣimit. Aseggas ur tettmassaṛ acemma. Msakit!
Ur ɛrin ara belli Aqbayli “alamma yesla i termegt i
yettcehid”, yebwa weglim-is, ur sen-yettaɣ ara awal alma
dayen tečča-t tezmert. ḥemdan yeɛra iman-is ur t-yuɣ
wara. Taferka-s tegguni-t, imeddukal-is ttračun-t ma d
icunga ines qurɛan-t, a t-iwet wugur ad llzen. Yebɣa a
sen-d-yesken imeḥḥa belli mazal-it d ḥemdan n zik u
tazmert ur t-tečči yara u ɣas yuṛen, tirrugza-s teqqim d
nettat. Yesteɛfa sin wussan…
Di lexḥif, deg wagur n Tubeḥ, yuɣ lṣal Furulu
yeffeɣ-d di lakul, yezga iteddu d babas ɣer lexla
Mmis n igellil
yettṣami-t-id di ccɣel. Uɣen-d tayuga n yezgaren, aɣyul d
wakraren. At wexxam akk dhan, yal wa d acu yeɛna. A s-tiniṛ uɣalen-d wussan n talwit. Yellez ḥemdan imi d-yufa
mmis ɣer yidis-is, d allal ɣef a yettkel. Yebɣa a s-yemmeslay am akken i wergaz, acku ɣures Furulu
yewweṛ d ilemɛi, mačči d aqcic nni n zik. A s-yehder ɣef
wayen t-yerṣan d azuzbu, qqimen deg wennar nnig
uɛecciw deg i mbabben idenyen n tazert. ḥemdan
yettxeḥḥiz tabarda ččan akk iɣerdayen asmi yella di Fḥansa.
- Twalaṛ a mmi, i s-d-yebda, lmal agi yakk nneɣ,
zemreɣ a d-aɣeɣ sin wakraren nniṛen. Aqlaɣ di sin
nezmer-asen. Di tefsut an-nezzenz tayuga yagi akken a d-naɣ tin meɛɛiyen. An-nezzenz daɣen tlata wakraren a d-nawi tafunast. Azemmur n useggwass-a a-d-yefk sennig
lɛula nneɣ ma yrad waṣnin. Deg unebdu, nek ad ttawiɣ
lxedḥa ɣer ssuq ɣef weɣyul, kečč d yessetmak a d-telhum
d lmal akked lexla. Syin a d-nbeddel aɣyul agi s userdun.
A tt-nerr i tnezzut, at-tedduṛ yidi ɣer leswaq iwakken at-tlemdeṛ. Ma tedda-tt akka, ma yehwa-yas i ḥebbi, ur
nettuɣal ara an-nellaɛ neɣ an-nenṣaf.
Simmal tefɣen-d imeslayen deg yimi n babas,
furulu itessiten; simmal yessefham-as-d amek yettwali
tameddit nnsen, aqcic yesmeṣsis yewhem. Tibbura s-d-yelli babas ur ttawint s anda yessaram, tikta n babas ur
teffiɣ fellas. Yesked deg yiman-is ad yuɣal d afellaṣ, a d-yessekcem tawant s axxam. Maca netta mačči akka i yɛer
iman-is, asirem-ines d ayen nniṛen. Yettwali-t deg
unelmad, d igellil maca d uṣric. Yennum tugna yagi n
unelmad, tezga ger wallen-is almi s-tekcem s ul-is,
iṣemmel-itt nezzeh. Atan babas di kra n dqayeq yesfeṛ Mulud Feraɛun i wid igellilen, ten-yesɛan,
asirem, iṛum kra yellan.
Akken ad yesnefsusi ɣef ul-is, yesbecbec-d seddaw tuɣmest:
- I limer a y-id-fken taggazt? Zemreɣ ad uɣaleɣ ɣer lakul mebla ma tserfeṛ felli duḥu. D ccix i yi-d-yennan.
Tamezwarut, ur tesɛiṛ i k-d-fkan taswiɛt agi, imi
tesriṣ yekfa yernu ur d ak-d-urin ara. Tin ɣers, ɣas
wwṛen-d yedrimen, tɣilleṛ i lakul umi nga nekkni? i taɣuri Nekkni d
yemḥkantiyen. Nutni zemren ad degḥen kra iseggasen, ad
xeṭren u taggara nnsen a tt-id-awin di taddart ad ttalin
ṭṭaren. Mačči akka i s-teṛra i mmis n Saɛid arehhan? Deg
Wegni, llan sin neɣ ma tlata akkagi. Steqsaɣ wwiɣ-d s
lexbar! Iḥumyen ur d-ttaken ara kan akka imukan,
yewɛer lṣal. Wamma ma teqqim yidi a d-tessiseṛ ayen a
d-ssiseɣ u wer d aɣ-yettxaṭ wara. Akka sin iseggasen neɣ
tlata a d-tawiṛ iman-ik, a d-timɣureṛ cwiṭ, syin at-zegreḍ ɣer Fḥansa. At-teɛreṛ dinna s tɣuri yagi inek, at-tɛaddiṛ
ansi k-yehwa, a tt-tselkeṛ ugar nneɣ. Ur ttɛeddint ara
fellak am akka ɛeddant fellaɣ. Tecbeṣ Fḥansa, teɛriṛ!
Aṭas n leṣwayeč a t-issineṛ, aṭas n tɣawsiwin a tlemdeṛ.
Asmi a d-taseṛ at-tiliṛ meqwreṛ, tewweṛ-d d argaz a k-d-nawi tameṭṭut. Atan amek ttwaliɣ ddunit. T-tagi i ɣ-ilaqen. Gmak a d-imed, a t-iliṛ s idis-is, a s-tbeddeṛ.
Yessetmak ad ddunt s ixxamen nnsent. At-tetfeṛ amṛiq-iw di kra yellan. Asenni xas mmuteɣ ad ḥuṣeɣ d afessas,
ttekleɣ ččiɣ-d argaz.
Yesmeṣsis Furulu u yufa-yas lbenna i wzeɣzen n
babas. D imeslayen n wemɣar azemni. Mi d-yudder babas
zwač, yebra i wqerru-s yuɣal wudem-is d azeggaɣ si
leṣya. ḥemdan ur d-yerfid ara allen-is ɣef tbarda
yettxeḥḥiz. Yekfa awal. Tasusmi ters-d, Furulu ur yesɛi d
acu a d-ileqqem deg wawal acku t-tusna d ṭṭwab i d-Mmis n igellil
yefɣen deg yimi n babas. Yalwa iwezzen imeslayen nni.
Yuɣal ḥemdan yessendeh mmis ɣef yiwen ccɣel, win
yuɣ-as awal yekker s leɛqel iḥuṣ.
Tameddit mi d-usan di lexla, ufan-d tabratt
tettraču Furulu. Tusa-d seg uɣerbaz n Tizi Wezzu, anda s
d-nnan belli taggazt tewweṛ-d u necden-t-id ad yas ad
yeṭṭef amṛiq t-yeggunin. Akka... ”Nekkni netṣebbir, ḥebbi yettṛebbir”.
Udem n weqcic ifeččeč, yefsex layas nni t-izedɣen,
yuɣal-as-d usirem. Tugna n unelmad igellil tennerna
cbaṣa ines, yennerna wazal-is. Yeṭṭef di targit-is am
mummu n tiṭ-is, tekcem-as s ul ladɣa tura mi tt-iwala
tteddu at-teffeɣ. Ula d babas s-timmad-is yenna-yas
waqila t-tidett, yumen. Aɛni d aɛeggun? Ad yanef i
tegwnitt am ta as-tenser, neɣ a s-nnesrent tmenṭac n alef
a d-yefk baylek i mmis yal aggur? Xaṭi! D ayen ibanen.
Ama d ḥemdan ama d mmis ur d-skeflen awal d-nnan di lexla. Ttun-t yemmut din. Rran-tt i wmeslay ṣaca
ɣef taggazt, taɣuri d uɣerbaz. Yennerna ccan n Furulu
tameddit nni, yessetmas qudḥent-tt mliṣ. Yemmas tekker ɣer imensi i lmend-is. Netta d babas ṭṭfen tiɣmert
ttmeslayen ɣef tɣawsiwin ten-yeggunin. Ilaq a d-heggin
lqec, mačči d ayen isehlen. Maca imi llan yedrimen deg
wexxam ur yelli uɛekkiḥ; “s uṭurdi, i s-yenna ḥemdan,
tiyersiwin fettint am waman n wedfel ass n-yiṭij”.
Azekka nni kan xemlen i yɣallen nnsen. ḥuṣen ɣer Tizi wezzu, ɛran-d anemhal n uɣerbaz, steqsan, u
Furulu yesser iman-is di lakul. Uznen ɣer Leããayer a d-aɣen isufar ilaqen. Îerfen aṭas n wedrim. Lqec amaynut
yusa-d, Furulu yewweṛ ɣer lebɣi-s. Ur d-yeqqim i Mulud Feraɛun
unelmad ṣaca anekcum s aɣerbaz. Yekfa wagur n Tubeḥ, tirga teffeɣ.
ḥemdan mačči d win sganayen. Yeɛra belli mmis
ur yettaweṛ sani n kra u wer d-yettawi acemma. Maca
yunef-as acku di temdint a yaf lqut aɛidan wala deg
wexxam, menyif din wala ma yeqqim di taddart ad
yettumarret am tezyiwin-is. Imi adabu yebɣa a s-d-yesker mmis, ḥemdan ur yugi yara. Yessaram kan ɣures,
a t-iwali yewweṛ d argaz, a t-id-iṣami deg usenker n
watmatenis d yessetmas.
Furulu di tama-s ur tt-yundi yara. S tidett-is i
yḥuṣ ɣer lakul. yebɣa ad iɣer seg ul iwakken a d-yeffeɣ d ccix.
Mmis n igellil
Asmi yeffeɣ Furulu axxam yeɣli-d rrehba. At
wexxam nneɣnin. Tameddit nni mi d-zzin i ymensi iban-d wemṛiq-is. Ixuṭ. Axxam meḥḥa a s-tiniṛ d ilem, neɣ
amzun meɛɛiyet twacult am akken netta weṣdes degs
tlata neɣ rebɛa iɛeggalen. Uɣalen a ttmeslayen fellas,
ṣala fellas. Yessetmas udrent-d akk tilufa sɛeddant ɣef
ilemɛi n gmatsent, ndemment imi s-ddant tikwal di
nneqma, ur ṭbirent ara i ymennuɣen-is, ur s-wwint ara;
ggullent ar sya ɣer zdat ar d as-ttaɣent awal ur ar t-ɛuzzent akken yuklal. Yemmas limmer tufi a s-t-ceggaɛ
tameɣbunt yeččan mmis yefferfer, yebɛed ɣef allen-is d
leṣnana ines. Ul-is yeččur, yedl-it leɣman. ḥemdan yebɣa
ad yekkes cwiṭ n lxiq i tmeṭṭut-is, maca mačči d ayen
yellan ger ifassen-is, ur yezmir ara. ččurent wallen n
Faṛma d imṭṭawen, netta yeggar-d nnhati, ikarreṛ-ed
taɣect-is snat neɣ tlata tikkal akken ad isebber iman-is.
U yernu, yehwa-yasen kan, Furulu atan di liser.
T-tikelt-is tamezwarut i yeṭṭes deg umeṭreṣ. Ayen yečča,
seg wakken igerrez u ɛid, ama d yemmas ama d
yessetmas ur zmirent at meyzent. Netta ur ten-id-yerri
yara yakk ger wallen-is. Yedder-iten ama akken di targit,
yerra-ten-id ɣer deffir a ten-iwali yiwen yiwen akken ur
s-yettensar wacemma degsen, u daɣen akken ad yekkes
aɣwbel t-tidett ayen iɛeddan fellas.
Ssebt tameddit: Deg wexxam i yella Furulu,
assen i s-d-wwṛen cwiṭ iceṭṭiden-is imaynuten. Deg
uɣerbaz bɣan a t-sersen ad yeggan din, babas yugi, acku
ilaq ad ixellleṭ, idrimen ulac aṭas. Yewqeɛ ḥemdan. Lqut Mulud Feraɛun
mačči d aɣwbel. I yiṛes? Yella si leɛṛil usensu, maca ad
yeskef akk cwiṭ uṭurdi nni yellan. D tawaɣit. Ad yečč
mmis di temdint weṣdes, ur yesɛi lwali ur yessin yiwen?
D awezɣi. A d-yerṛel ayen i wakken ad iqbel taluft n
tguni n mmis? Terwi. U yernu anemhal n lakul yenna-yas-d d win kan i d ixef-is.
Lṣed taṭebṣit: Ddunit am lmeṭbaṣ, tettaɣ txetti.
Tuɣ-d ɣer Furulu deg wudem yedhen sser n Aɛzir. Aɛzir
t-tizya-s, nat Wegni. Deg uɣerbaz i ɣer a yekcem Furulu i
deg i yeqqar. Yesla s Furulu fkan-as-d taggazt yusa-d
ɣures ɣer Tizi ad iqeṭṭer yides. D acaɛlal, d azemḥaq u
yezga wudem-is yecreh, yeṛsa, mačči d win mi yekres
wenyir. Ur yezzi ur yenniṛ deg wawal:
- Ula d nek am keč, i s-yenna i Furulu, Aqli deg
uɣerbaz n Tizi Wezzu anda akken tserseṛ iman-ik. Din i
qqareɣ. Ɣer yiwet n temda i ngerr iman nneɣ. Ma tebɣiṛ
an-nedukkul akken, aɛyiɣ weṣdi. Aqlaɣ deg yiwet n
tmurt an-nemwanas meqqar.
Yebɣa ad yemmeɣ ɣer temgarṭ-is Furulu, a s-d-yemṣilleq. Waqila yusa-d win a yefsin tiyersi? send a d-yenṭeq Furulu win yerna-yas-d:
n tguni inu di lakul.
Yella di Tizi Wezzu yiwen wexxam mi qqaren
tuɣṛat. Yezga-d kan ɣer rrif n uɣerbaz. Ttaṭafen din arrac
igellilen d-iṭubben deg wedrar akken ad ɣren. Nek din i
zedɣeɣ. Azal n tlatin yidneɣ i nella. Hedḥeɣ-asen fellak.
Ɣurneɣ taxxamt, ṭṭabla, ikersiyen d sin yemṭerṣen. Yal
ṭṭbeṣ ttaken-aɣ-d tacrift akked weɣrum. U yernu annect-a yakk baṭel.
D ayen ur nkeččem deg wallaɣ. Aɛzir yesfehma-s-d belli win yeṭfen tuɣṛat d argaz bu lxir, yettṣami
igellilen am wemḥabeṛ uḥumi. Yal tameddit a ten-id-- Baba mačči d ameḥkanti akken ad yernu ameṭruf
Mmis n igellil
yessemlil ɣer yiwet n tzeqqa a sen-d-yemmeslay ɣef ddin,
ɣef ttrebga. Itelli-yasen allen nnsen ɣef ddunit, lṣaṭun,
yemmal-asen iberdan yelhan. Yefreṣ Furulu, d lemziyya
tameqrant. Imiren kan yeqbel. Yuɣal yenna-yas-d Aɛzir s
wacu a yeglu lqec, idrimen, idlisen, mi s-d-ihedder,
furulu yunag wallaɣ-is. Fkan ttiɛad i wzekka nni di
tafrara. Syen yerra s axxam a d-iheggi ayen a yawi.
Yekkes taɛkumt i babas mi s-yessaweṛ asal ɣef i wer
yebni. ḥemdan, di tama-s, bessif i yumen ayen s-d-iṣekku mmis. D leɛčeb! ḥebbi wer yečči yiwen!
Yerkeb Furulu di tkeḥḥust i tikkelt tamezwarut! T-targit
neɣ t-tidett? Yerra qbala ɣer lakul, mebla ma yɛedda ɣer
mas Lambert, aqerru n wexxam n tuɣṛat. ɛarqent-as ger
wannecten n warrac. Ur yeɛqil ara iman-is. Yelsa akustim
am wiyaṛ akk. Send ad kecmen ɣer lakul, acku qqimen
deg umḥaṣ ttawin ttarran, yusa-d ɣures Aɛzir iṭeggem-as
takrabaṭ-is, netta yessen... Yiwen ur s-d-igir tamawt.
Yedduri tacdaṭ n wemdakkel-is. Tikwal tettali-t-id tezweɣ
s udem-is mebla sseba. Yeggugem, yugi a t-id-yali
wawal. Kra n warrac xemsen yides, sseddan-t-id mi
xemsen i Aɛzir. Mi kecmen ɣer tzeɣwa qqimen ad ɣren,
allen-is berqent, yesmusul akka n wakka. Ddmen-d
warrac tikaḥniyin ula d netta yeddem-d, llin idlisen iga
am nutni, ṭṭafaren ayen d-teqqar tcixett ula d netta
yesmeṣsis, ayen xeddmen akk iɛuned-iten, iṣun ḥebbi,
yiwen ur s-ifaq. Yiwen ur t-id iwala ddaw tiṭ. Ssaɛa
tamezwarut tmerret-it. Yeqbeḥ, mačči d wagi i d amḍiq-is. Ahbuh! I keč a yameksa lakul agi s ṭṭiqan n djaj, s
ṭwabel timaynutin yettberriqen? I keč tezdeg agi a
ykukru bab-is a tt-yessimes? Ɣef ddemma-k i d-tusa
tcixett inna tuzyint yettmeslayen s ttawil, s yiles aɛidan,
yessefhamen s wecmumeṣ, yesteqsayen s lemqadra? Mulud Feraɛun
Tuklaleṛ tiɣimit ger warrac nni s lqec nnsen azedgan,
amaynut, s leṣdaqa nnsen? Tetti ddunit ɣef Furulu, a s-tiniṛ t-tukerṛa i d-yuker amṛiq-is garasen. Allen n Aɛzir,
tikwal ma d-rsent fellas, s tmuɣli nni ines tacmamaṣt,
qqarent-as-d wer ttaggad. Acṣal teṣma tmuɣli nni! Ayen
meqqret lemziyya n Aɛzir! Ɣef lɛecra, mi d-ffɣen cwiṭ ɣer wemraṣ, yettenkaɛ degs ukukru s-icudden imi.
Sumata, ass amezwaru, ṣedqen akk warrac garasen. Ma
wid ur neqqar yides ur t-id-walan ara yakk, amzun ulac-it, wiyaṛ  kra degsen  ttnecraṣen yides akken a t-id
sneṭqen: Wa yesmesxir akken a t-id-yesseṛs, wayeṛ
yerra iman-is yessefhamm-d am akken txededem tcixett,
ma d yiwen yessefruy am deg umezgun. ččuren-as akk tiṭ
i Furulu, iṣemmel-iten meḥḥa. Yettwali iman-is meɛɛi
garasen, yezder, d ulac. Yeṣqer iman-is!
Ɣef leṣdac, dduklen netta d Aɛzir. Ffɣen ɣer beḥḥa
ččan-d imekli lexmis, aṛebsi n lbaṭaṭa, aksum d sin
ifarrawen n claṛa, T-tameɣra ɣures! maca d aneɛruṛ kan
i yeɛreṛ, ur yelluɛ ara. Yerwa lferṣ.
Ɣef rrebɛa t-tirza ɣer mas Lembert.
D argaz ameqran, lqedd-is yebded, ma yleṣṣu a
s-tiniṛ d aɛsekriw. Terna-yas lhiba tamart-is, snernan-as
ccan imeslayen-is uwzinen. D ṭṭwab i d-tefɣen di taɣect
nni ines tazurant, d nniya i d-yettfuḥḥun deg wudem-is, d
leṣnana i d-yettaɣen di tmuɣli-s. Tuggdin n tazwara ttetti
d laman. A s-taɣeṛ awal ma ur d ak-yehwi, at-tedduṛ yides
ma ur tebɣiṛ. Ak-idel s tiɛet n yiles-is a s-tefkeṛ “aɛuɣer”.
Yal aqcic di lakul yeɛra taɛkumt iɛebba. Âɛayet, ladɣa ma
tteɛmaden agus imawlan-is akken ur s-yettak ara wul-is
ad yessedrem asirem n wid yetteklen fellas. Ma d wid
yellan ɣer Mas Lembert mačči akken i ttwalin tamsalt.
Nutni ɣursen yiwen weɣbel: fellasen a s-ddun di lebɣi.
Ma uɣen-as awal, ddan-as di lebɣi, yellez yissen ulamek a
Mmis n igellil - Xaṭi.
- Igerrez. Heṛr-iyi-d kan cwiṭ ɣef at wexxam
nneɣnin imawlan n weqcic. Yeṭṭef amṛiq n ccix-is, n
babas, n wemdakkel-is n wurar i kra n win “d-yeggujlen”
ɣures. Yeččur-as tiṭ i Furulu u ters fellas nniya-s:
- d keč i d Furulu? - Ih.
- Iheṛr-iyi-d fellak Aɛzir. Yides a tzedɣeṛ di
texxamt. Attan thegga. At-tuɣaleṛ at-tennameṛ axxam agi
nneɣ. Asmuncef xaṭi! Yak ur ttesseṛ ara ddexxan meqqar? nnwen.
Yemmeslay-as-d Furulu ɣef ayen akk iwala deg
wexxam nnsen: amek ttidiren, d acu i sɛan d wayen i ten-ixuṭṭen. Yefhem Mas Lembert belli yeɣli-yas umeɣbun
nniṛen ɣer irebbi. Anef!
- Tesɛiṛ taggazt, t-tin i d ṭṭeṣ. Ilaq-ak at-tṣeḥceṛ
akken ur k-tt-tekksen ara. Imdukal-ik meḥḥa wwin-d iman
nnsen. Ɣurek ha! - Ih.
- Dagi, at-tuɣaleṛ d askuti.
- Ih, i s-yenna Furulu mebla ma yxemmem.
- At-tuɣaleṛ at-teɛreṛ d acu-t sya ɣer zdat.
S wawal aɛidan i msefḥaqen. Deg wassenni yuɣal
Furulu d aɛeggal n twacult n “Nat Lembert”. Yers-d liser!
Tameddit nni aṭas n yeskutiyen i d-yemlal, iqesseḥ
yidsen, yufa-ten ur d iriten ara.
Atan amek yezri wass amezwaru. Send ad yeṭṭes
yerra-t-id ɣer deffir am usaru. Yefreṣ, yeṣmed ḥebbi.
Ma ur d-yemmekti yara aṭas gmas, yessetmas d imawlan-is, Akli, amdakkel-is n temɛi yerra-t-id ger wallen-is, Mulud Feraɛun
yečča-t-in d ameksa di tmurt. Ma d netta, Furulu...
lṣara yettuɛerben, yiwet n
iɛeṭṭel ara Furulu yezwi ɣef
Axxan n tuɣṛat n Mass Lembert yezga-d di tama
ufella n temdint, anagar abrid i t-yebṛan d uɣerbaz.
Idisan-is ɣursen azal n settin n lmitrat.
Deg yiwet n teɣmert tella tnezduɣt n bab-is, ɣer
tama-s d lčamaɛ iḥumyen, t-tazeqqa tameqrant. Tixxamin
n warrac ṭṭfent yiwen yidis: setta ukessar, setta usawen.
Tesɛa yiwet n tebṣirt
yettuṣerzen nezzeh, yiwet n temda yentellen, sin yeɛricen
d snat n tseddaḥin. Atan wexxam deg i yesɛedda Furulu d
wemdakkel-is Aɛzir rebɛa isegwasen; Dagi i stumnen i
lxedma nnsen u mecṣen tiɛeṭ n wayen d-megren, dagi i tuyat-is Ur
teɛda tdukli garasen, tin mi wer yezmir wakud a tt-iceqqeq acku temsel s lemqadḥa u tedhen s leṣmala tafessast.
timṣeqranit iɛebba s ufus-is, tin s-yeskawen ifadden u s-yettlen iles. Yesfeṛ deg wallaɣ-is tikti ssi yessezder iman-is ger yemdukal-is. Degmi ten-iwala mačči d wid
“yessafagen taɣuri“, ixeddem s lmul almi d-yewwi iman-is. Yeṣḥes iman-is am netta am wemdakkel-is Aɛzir ur
ten-iɣaṛ ara lṣal, ur sen-ṭṭifen ara taṣsift, ɛran mačči d
rregmat. Účan-ten nnan; deg yimir ufan lehna.
Yal ass n lṣed teddun d mass Lembertg ɣer teɛgi
ttelmaden amek a qqlen d iskutiyen. Furulu yewhem,
amek argaz ameqran am agi yettṛeggir lweqt-is di temsal
am tigi ur nesɛi lmaɛna? Ɣef akka yettwali, ula d
imeksawen n wedrar d iskutiyen ur ɛrin iman nnsen!
Ayen yeɛnan iṭudaf n tsekkutit, ur tesɛiṛ a sen-d-tessukseṛ. Askuti n tidett ɣures azal. Di tazwara, Furulu d
wemdakkel-is ṣman, iɛčeb-iten lṣal, maca cwiṭ cwiṭ
qqlen fsin ladɣa mi faqen ṭṭuqtent tkerkas di kra n
yeskutiyen tt-yettarran i wkellex d nnṣas. Di taggara
Mmis n igellil
tufɣa n wass n lṣed tettas-ed sennig wul. Rɛaget u ɛɛayet ɣer sin imesdurar nni. Werčin nudan a d-ifriren. D lakul
kan i d aɣbel nnsen. Mass Lembert ifaq-asen, maca ur
ten-yeṣḥis ara, ur sen-yenni yara ad xedmen nnig tezmert
nnsen. Imi tgerrez tikli nnsen yellez.
Ur xeddmen ara s lmul ula timeddiyin ma ara
mlilen d warrac nniṛen di tzeqqa nni rran d lčamaɛ
iḥumyen. ḥwaṣ zgan ttḥuṣun, qqaren-d am yemdukal
nnsen yiwet n tṭurett, cennun am nitni, ttaken tameɛɛuɣt
maca mi d-fɣen kan syin qbala ɣer texxamt nnsen ad gren
iqerray nnsen deg yedlisen t-tkaḥniyin. Ula d yibbas ur
ten-iwala yiwen rran s Amrabeṛ Uḥumi a sen-d-yefk
ddeɛwa n lxir, neɣ a t-steqsin a sen-d-yessefru taṭurett. S
lferṣ i d-yessefham mass Lembert timsal n ddin i wid d-yettasen ɣures, llan kra degsen seg ul, kra teddun-as di
lebɣi i wemɣar. Aɛzir d Furulu ur ten-yeɛri ula d abrid
usan-d, nsern-as, ifaq ur ten-id-yettawi yara yides.
Tadukli nnsen terna kra yellan, ur yezmir yiwen a ten-yebṛu. Ur smaɛḥiqen, ur kḥihen ddin Iḥumyen ur yezdiɣ
kra n ddɣel deg ulawen nnsen. D lakul nnsen kan i ten-yerṣan. Seg wakken zgan ttḥuṣun ɣer tɛallit, tkeččem
leṣnana n ddin deg ulawen nnsen. Wwṛen almi lemden
Tikwal ma ttdekkiḥen
nnesxa iḥumyen am aman.
weṣedsen yettaɛčab-iten lṣal, ttawin-d icewwiqen deg i
d-ttaddren ɛissa. Ttɛallan s tufra, tikwal, am akken
xedmen yemdukal nnsen.
Sennig taɣuri nnsen ulac i yesɛan azal ger wallen-nnsen. Zedɣen di tuɣṛat akken ad afen iman nnsen, ad
ɣren di liser. Lebɣi nnsen ṭṭfen degs, asirem nnsen
meqqer. Sɛeddan tanubit nnsen, si xemseṭṭac almi d
tmenṭac iseggasen, ur msebṛan. Zzgan am iṛudan n ufus.
D isegwasen nni n tnubit i ymettlen argaz, d wid i d lemri
n tmeddit n wemdan. Deg uzal atnan di lakul, tameddit Mulud Feraɛun
mi d-fɣen ɣer wemrabeṛ Uḥumi kfan taɛallit ttarran ɣer
texxamt. Qqaren ɣer teftilt alma d lɛecra, acku di tuɣṛat
snusuyen tiftilin lawan nni, syin ad ssiɣen tacemmaɛt ad
ɛiwzen ɣer tafat-is akked yedlisen nnsen alma d azgen n
yiṛ neɣ ugar. Tikwal tettifrir-d tafat nitni ur teqqin tiṭ
nnsen, sellan-as, ɣer yiwet n taddart nnigsen, i ccix n
lčamaɛ ma ara d-yadan ccix.
Awah! Uṛan n tegrest ad asen-ccfun! Tasusmi
tdel axxam, teɣli-d am buberrak. Ala aṛu yettsuṛun di
beḥḥa d ugeffur yekkaten i wumi ara a tselleṛ. Ddunit
meḥḥa teṭṭes! Ger cqayeq n ṭṭaq teffɣen-d kra izigen n
tafat di texxamt nnsen. T-tacemmaɛt i yreqqen. Nutni
qqimen, mqabalen, nnṛen deg yebranyas, tikaḥniyin d
yedlisen zdatsen. Yiwen ur yettmeslay i wayeṛ. Dhan i
sin di tɣuri. ttnaɣen d yiman nnsen akken ur ten-irennu
ɛɛayit, iqerra cuffen. Seqḍen deg yemdukal nnsen tt-yewwten d iṛes. Ɣas akken ur fkin taqejjirt ɣer deffir.
Rebɛa iseggasen meḥḥa, nutni d amerret. Werǧin ḥuṣen ɣer lakul mebla ma lemden ayen sen-d-yefka ccix, neɣ
mebla ma tteklen ɣef yiman nnsen. Asmi yewweṛ Furulu
s aɣerbaz amagnu, anda ur yeṣwač ara ad ineɣ iman-is di
tɣuri, ifaq belli, kra n teswiɛin, imaṣṣen di rrayaɛ u t-tikli
iṛegger tadawsa ines di ɛawaz.
Nnig ameṣṣen ḥwan di tɣuri nnsen, tteɛmaden agu
u ttcuṣun ɣef t-ɛabbaṛ nnsen. Ibɣun weṭṭin yedlisen ɣef
tdawsa, ɣef lqut lɛali, ɣef wayen i ylaq a t-yečč ilemɛi
akken ad yawi iri, ad yimɣur u ad yuzur ufud-is, ur sen-ikeččem sya ur sen-iteffeɣ sya. Lqut nnsen n yal ass d
lbaṭata, ḥaca lbaṭata! Uɣen-d aricu, sebbwayen di
texxamt. Lbaṭata teshel i wsebwi u bninet. Ayen tt-iṣemmel Furulu! Maca, akken ɛeddan sin iseggasen,
limmer yettaf ur t-yettwali yara. Ma d Aɛzir, ma
Mmis n igellil
temmugremt-id yibbwas, addert-as-d awal n lbaṭata at-teɛrem “tameɣra” a wen-ig! Tikwal i wakken ad beddlen
imekli, tetten di berra lqut asemmaṛ. Azgen n weɣrum di
sin yidsen rennun-as asafar si zrrin yess d-ttaɣen s ɛecra
neɣ xemseṭṭac n duru. Di tmenṭac n alef d-ttaṭafen yal
aggur, yal yiwen yettṣerif degsent tmanya alaf. ɛecra alaf
nniṛen d-iggarrin ttaken-tent s axxam.
Tikwal akka, Ṛemḍan d dda Muṣend, babas n
Aɛzir, rezzun-d fellasen u gganen ɣursen. Ferṣen di sin d
warraw nnsen imi ttcuṣun, ṣerrzen, ur llin d wid mi
qqeḥsen lečyub. Ladɣa ḥemdan yellez nezzeh.
Di taddart ala ayen yelhan i ttmeslayen ɣef
Furulu. Ziɣen lakul ur isekkef ara idrimen, ur itett ara di
texriṭ n ḥemdan maca tallalt n mmis di ccɣel txuṭ-it, ur
yufi wukud a d-yemṣami ddunit. Ula t-tayuga n yezgaren
terna-t, ur yezmir ara a tt-iqam, yewweṛ almi tt-yezzenz,
yelha-d ṣaca t-tferkiwin. Deg unebdu, ma d-yawi tesriṣ
Furulu, ttɛuzzun-t deg wexxam, yettbuddu-t ḥemdan xir
n wakken ttbuddun wiyaṛ arraw nnsen imeksawen:
Afenčal n tecrift yal ṭṭbeṣ, seksu n ssmid ur tiswiɛin
yettenfaq-ed i lmend-is. At wexxam stumnen i lqut nni
aɛidan, ufan ɣers, nnumen-t, ma t-taɛzzult tettafeg. Asmi
d-yewweṛ lawan i deg a yessɛeddi Furulu di lezzayer,
iseyyef lṣal babas a d-yerṛel akken a s d-yaɣ akustim u a
s-yernu cwiṭ umesḥuf. Di tazwara, ikukra ḥemdan ad
yerhen tazemmurt neɣ snat almi ymeyyez yufa belli s
yedrimen nni, ahat, ar a yessufeɣ leɛtab n mmis ɣer tafat
ur t-ɣaṛent ara. Yerna kra n wagguren yeɣli-yas-d
umesḥuf yuɣal s areṭṭal nni. Teqqel-as t-tannumi. Yeɛya
deg umerret, ɣlin ifadden-is, yebra i yman-is umeɣbun;
Ddunit ṣercawet, netta yekkaw. Di taggara, yesnefsusuy
taɛkumt n twacult s-yuɣalen t-taɛayant s ureṭṭal. Ibub Mulud Feraɛun
ṭṭlaba am teɛrurt. S ilaɛṛil, ar d-yas lawan, att-yesres ɣef
tuyat tileqqaqin n Furulu.
Mmis n igellil
Di lawan i deg imedukal deg i yeqqar lhan-d d
ucebbaṣ akked zzhu t-tullas, Furulu yerra ddehn-is ṣaca i
tɣuri ines. Lṣif deg i xbabṛen at wexxam nnsen ur s-yelli
di labal. Ɣef seṭṭac iseggasen yetturar s ddunit-is akw t-tmeddit-is s tusnakt.
Yettɣiṛi-t lṣal, itett-it wul-is u yettaṭaf taṣsift.
ččan tasa-s warraw n taddart-is ur nettkil ara fellas akked
wid yeskaɛriren ɣef
twacult-is. Yekfa aseggas-is
amezwaru n tɣuri di Tizi Wezzu, anda d-yewwi iman-is
nezzeh, aqrib t-id-sṭaxren. Kksen-as taggazt, yiwen ur
yeɛri ayɣer. Anemhal yurča aggur, sin, ur d-yewwiṛ
wacemma. Di taggara n Dujember yessufeɣ-d meḥḥa wid i
wumi ur d-tusi taggazt-is. Yers-d leṣzen deg wexxam n
ḥemdan amzun t-tanṭelt. Ačabi n yedrimen i wakken ad
yuɣal weqcic ɣer lakul, ad yesnerni di tɣuri ines, ɣas ur t-id-ttader ara! Yiwen ur t-id-igir ger wallen-is. Meḥḥa
nnan-as belli Furulu dayen ad yeṣbes, yidneɣ a yeqqim,
taggara-s t-tayessawt. Sseqṛen-t-id umeɣbun, ma t-tura
ilaq-as ad yelli allen-is ad iwali tidett am lemri.
Akken kan a yɛaddi umenzu n Yennayer, ad
yekfu tesriṣ, ad bdun di taddart tiyita di Furulu, anda ar a
yeddu a t-ṛefren s uṛad. Yugad dayen txemmimen at-taddart a s-d-yeṛrun. S tufra i yettru umeɣbun, ur yezmir
a d-yeffeɣ ɣer beḥḥa, isetṣa am win mi d-ssuksen. U
yernu mačči t-tiṣeḥci ur yeṣḥic ara mi t-id-sṭaxren, d
adrim i yulaṣed. Yeggul-asen uemhal di lakul ar d ad
yaru ɣer lezzayer, yenna-yasen-d belli t-tatut kan a yettun
neɣ d aɛraq i ɛerqen. Amek, ad kksen taggazin i warrac
meḥḥa? D lmuṣal! Maca wizemren a sen-d-yessefhem
akka di taddart? Mulud Feraɛun
iɛer yiwen. Wid
- Fkan-ak-d rrkel a mmis n ḥemdan, ah! Ggran-- Rrčut kan at-teɛrem ma ur uɣaleɣ ara!
- S werhan n tferka n babak ma yefka ḥebbi?
- I keč tuqɛa-k-d? Dacu a k-id-yegren?
- Aṣlil a mmi! Ad yili ḥebbi yidek. I wakken a d-Ddurt nni n tesriṣ, yessɛadda-tt meḥḥa Furulu di
Tizi Wezzu. Ur yebɣi ad
t-id-yettmagaren smuɣbunen yess, ala win a s yinin aṣlil.
Yečča-t wul-is. D acu
tebɣiṛ! “Imawlan ṭebren,
immɛazzan kefren”. Win mi yḥuṣ a d-yessefhem belli ur
t-id-sṭaxren ara di lakul, t-taggazt i yɛeṭlen ur d-tewwiṛ
ara, ussan agi kan a s tt-id-rren, ad yetthuccu aqerru-s.
Yiwen yugi a s-d-yefk tameɛɛuɣt. Am win iceṭṣen i
wderɣal. Ttaččaren-t-d wallen-is d imeṭṭawen s wurfan, ttarran-t t-taṛsa.
ak-d wussan akk t-ɣeṭṭen am nekkni!
tṣamiṛ babak atan yekfa, a t-tzelluṛ s yiccer.
Ula d babas tenquqel-as nniya, yendem mi d-yenjer i mmis abrid ur nessufuɣ, abrid d-yettuɛerben i
win yellan d igellil.
Ussan n-yeqqim Furulu di Tizi rɛagit. Yezga
yexḥeb wudem-is. Imeɛɛuɣen-is ddubzen deg mennan,
tettquddur tasa-s mi ywala tismin izedɣen medden. Tuɣal-as ddunit t-taberkant, uɣalen-as akk lɣaci am qedḥan. Ur
yufi d acu a s-yekksen lxiq. Cwiṭ cwiṭ yuɣal ifaq belli
tismin nni nat taddart, tukḥin nnsen, taṛsa nni nnsen
tasellawt kkant-ed seg wakken tteklen fellas, umnen s
lakul ines u taggara kra din yeddem-it waṛu, kra din ur d-iban. Ɣillen yewweṛ-d lawan i deg a d-yerfed at Musa, a
ten-id-yessufeɣ deg udaynin ɣer tɣerɣert, a ten-id-yssukes
deg umejḥiw, a sen-yesfeṛ lṣif, Ziɣen…
Asmi d-tusa di Tizi Wezzu tebratt d-yeglan s usal
n lɛali, tuɣal-it-id teḥwiṣt, iṣar ad yuɣal ɣer lakul. Yeggul
Mmis n igellil
ar d ineɣ d iman-is alma yrebṣ-ed. Tenna-yas yemmas ad
ssufɣeɣ lwaɛda i tqubbett n taddart, maca netta yeɛra
mačči d lwaɛda a s d-yellin tibbura neɣ a t-yessiwṛen ɣer
lebɣi-s. ḥaca dderɛ-is, anagar tamusni-s ar a t-iwansen.
Ma akken ttelmaden yemkukal-is isefra n tayri, netta
yettruɛu aqerru-s deg wid sen-d-yettak ccix, yettelmad-iten am aman. Ma ara d-yekker a ten-id-iɣer, yettɣawal u
yettɛeggiṛ di lbidal a ten-id-iɣer s taɣect ṣlawen i sen-iwulmen, s ttawil, ladɣa ccix a d-isuɣ fellas, a t-id-yerr s
abrid, Furulu ad yenneɣni, ad yekres anyir-is ad yessusem.
Ur yeɛri Furulu amek a yexdem i wakken a d-yessukes imarrawen-is deg waluṛ deg xnunsen, di lṣif
ten-izelfen. Akken yebɣu yili, ur s-yefki yara wul-is ad
yefcel, yeɛra belli “Wibɣan ad yɣellet yefk laɛtab i ufus-is”, dderk yefka-t, ma d aɣellet ilaq ad iɣellet i yebɣun
yeṛru. Asmi d-yerbeṣ, tawacult-is twala belli ur iṛegger
ara ḥebbi tidi-s, ula d at taddart faqen belli mačči i wurar
i wumi tt-yerra. Ɣas akkenni irebṣ-ed yegguni-t uzazwer,
acku asirem n Furulu d anekcum s aɣerbaz amagnu akken
a d-yeffeɣ d ccix.
Yal aseggas, deg unebdu, yettas-ed ɣer tmurt.
Tessusuf-it-id temdint s adrar, netta itezzi-yas s weɛrur
itettu-tt. Tjebbed-it taddart cwiṭ cwiṭ: tajmaɛt, lqahwa,
tizyiwin-is akked ccɣel n lexla ttaran-t d amessedrar.
Ma ara yekfu tesḥiṣ, a s-tiniṛ mačči d win n-yeččan
tamdint i yuɣalen ɣures, yettaɛraq ula i warrac deg i
yeqqar, acku amzun akken yessenṭel taglimt-is, sneclen-t
izilan u tesseɣr-it lxedma.
Yeggra-yas-d i Furulu yiwen useggas. D aseggas-is aneggaru deg uɣerbaz! Yuɣal a t-id-yernu. Lṣala nat
wexxam nnsen rqiqet, werčin ten-terni ddunit am webrid
agi, tessaṣnunef-iten. Di taddart yuɣ-ed leqdeḥ s ufus-is, Mulud Feraɛun
- ḥuṣ a mmi, a k-d-yelli ḥebbi tibbura n lxir. A k-mačči d aqcic nni n zik. Tamsalt yellan yettcawaḥ-it fellas
babas; agraw d-yegren ssawalen-as-d leɛmum-is d xwal-is a s-yeṣdeḥ, tibratin mi swaɛren medden ɣures i d-ttasen. Aṭas i s-d-ṣekkun tamedḥurt nnsen, yettak-asen
lɛaqliyya-s, tamusni-s. Ssulin-as azal, rnan-as ccan, netta
ur yessemɣar ara iman-is. Limmer d lebɣi-k a yul ad yaf
tayett i ɣer a ysenned, win a t-iweṭṭin, a s-yesnefsusi
taɛkumt, a s-d-yefken ḥḥay-is a yeṛfer s tuqna n wallen.
Limmer yufi a d-yelhu kan d weɣbel-is, d lakul-is. Send
ad yeṭṭef abrid-is, yenna-yas babas:
yawi ḥebbi d webrid.
ččurent-ed wallen n yemmas d imeṭṭawen mi
temsalam yides, tesself-as i wudem-is, temṣalleq-as,
tefreṣ yess. Iban yiṭij uzal. Imarrawen-is ur cukken ara
degs. Tteklen, uɣen tannumi, mmitsen a d-yerbeṣ taɣuri
ines am laɛwayed-is. Tikkelt agi, ɛran daɣen a ten-id-yessefreṣ.
Netta ɣures lexbar limmer a s-yenser uzazwar
asegwas-a, tibbura uɣerbaz amagnu ad medlent fellas, ur
s-ttanef ara a s-yales qabel acku yessaweṛ di laɛmeḥ. Ilaq-as daɣen ad yeṣḥes iman-is. Ur sent-d-tus ara di lbal i
ymarrawen-is belli ma yexṭer tikkelt-a a tt-id-yečč di Fḥansa. Anebdu i
yettxemmim. Din tella lxedma, wamma ma yeqqim di
Lezzayer yewqaɛ ger sin iberdan: ad yuɣal d ccix, atan
yekfa ḥebbi ɣef imawlan-is lṣif, ma ulac a tt-yerr i
tyessawt, ayen yeɣra ad iḥuṣ am waman n wedfel.
Simmal zerrin wussan yettban-as-d uzazwar i
Furulu am uwaɣziw, yeswaɛr-it. Simmal yeqqar
yettefcal? Yettmeyyiz weṣdes asmi a d-yas ɣer taddart
deg unebdu i d-teddun, s yedlisen ur ten-nfiɛ, a t-id-temmager yemmas s imeṭṭi babas s wudem n lmegget.
iɛeddan meḥḥa ɣef wannect-a
Mmis n igellil
Ɣas yemmas at-tettru at-teqqel a s-tsuref, ma d babas a
tent-yaɣ ɣer daxel ad yeqbeḥ. Lɣaci nniṛen a d-sqeṛɛen
iles nnsen ɣer ttiha sennig tamuɣli nnsen n ddaw tiṭ.
Tiswiɛin yeyyal-it-id lṣamu yettačar wul-is d asirem.
Yettuɣal-it-id ḥḥuṣ: Ɣef tayett-is i d-senden at wexxam
nnsen, fellas i tebna tmeddit nnsen, ger ifassen-is i tella
tifrat iɣeblan nnsen. Akka i yettwali tamsalt ddurt send
ass n wessɛaddi. Isub-d babas ɣer Tizi Wezzu, yewwi-yas-d cwiṭ n yedrimen i wmesḥuf-is di Lezzayer. Mi d
lawan ad yali ɣer taddart, iwunes-it Furulu almi d anda a
yerču akamyun a d-iɛeddin a t-yawi.
- Di Lezzayer a t-ssɛaddim, i s-yenna babas, yernu
aṭas yidwen i tellam. Ad fernen kan kra garawen. Yettiki
zzheḥ, teɛriṛ? Keč a t-tṭubbeṛ ɣer Lezzayer, nekkni deg
wedrar a k-nerču. a d-tuɣaleṛ s axxam xas ur d-terbiṣeṛ
ara. Err di labal-ik belli i yebɣun yili, aɛzizeṛ fellaneɣ. U
yernu, yella wizemren a k-yekkes ayen teɣriṛ? Tura nek ugadeɣ ara.
ad aliɣ s axxam. A s-iniɣ i yemmak belli nemɛer. A sen-iniɣ daɣen belli ur tugadeṛ ara.
- Ɣas kkes-asen ɣef wul iwsawen, in-asen ur Mulud Feraɛun Amawal: Addud Afna Agacur Agim
Agul, ttl. igulen Ahanay Ahareg Akayad
Akerdis, ttl. ikerdisen Triangle Alameɣ Allal Amagnu Aɣerbaz amagnu Amaras
Amarraw, ttl. imarrawen Amenzay Amerray Amerwas Amejjay Ameɛɛul
Amkuɛ, ttl. imkuɛen
Amrig, ttl. imrigen Amyag Amɛiw Anamek
Asaṛ, ttl. isaṛen Aseklu Aselkim Asentel Hẓrǧs Arbre Certificat ThAme Niḍɛau
Aswir, ttl. Iswiren Attitude Adḍersaire Hasard Mille Erreur Sttectacle Gymnastique Examen Luxe Mǧyen Nǧrmale ẓcǧle nǧrmale Candidat reõu Parent Princitte Tǧuriste Dette, deḍǧir Medecin Lǧgique Carrẓ Arme Verbe Mǧnstre Sens, exttlicatiǧn.
Axanab, ttl. ixanaben Azaraf Azazwar Aɛeɣzen Ccil Iba Immal Inaw Ini Suqel Tadawsa Tafekka Taggazt Tallalt Tamendit Tameɛla Tamtarwit
Tamsirt, ttl. timsirin Tanezzut
Tanfalit, ttl. tinfaliyin Tanubit
Tarrayt, ttl. Tirrayin Tasekla
Tawinest, ttl. tiwinas Tugna Tuɣdaṭ Ussis Wennet Yugda Yesɛan inzeɣ

Mulud Feraɛun ilul ass n 12 mars
1913 di Tizi-Hibel. Di
1946, Feraɛun yuɣal d aselmad di
Tewrirt Musa mbaεd mi d-yeffeɣdeg
uɣerbaz n Buzariɛa. Di 1952, Yuɣal d
anemhal n uɣerbaz n Larba nat
Iraten. Di 1957, Feraɛun yeffeɣsi
tmurt n Leqbayel, iṛuḥ ar Lezzayer
anda yeṭṭef aɣerbaz Nadǧr di Clǧs-Salembier.
Ger wayen yura Mulud Feraɛun:
Mmmis n igellil, Akal d yidim, Iberdan
yessawnen, Ussan di tmurt, aɣmis
55-62, Tibratin i yemddukal-is, Amuli.
Yettwanɣa Feraɛun s ṛṣaṣ n lOAS
netta akked xemsa yemddukal-is ass
